# Import necessary libraries
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler

# Step 1: Loading the dataset
url = "https://archive.ics.uci.edu/ml/machine-learning-databases/00597/garments_worker_productivity.csv"
data = pd.read_csv(url)

# Handling missing values
data['wip'] = data['wip'].fillna(data['wip'].mean())

# Step 2: Transform the target variable into a binary class label
threshold = 0.7  # Threshold for satisfactory productivity
data['class_label'] = np.where(data['actual_productivity'] >= threshold, 1, 0)

# Step 3: Visualize feature distributions (optional)
data.hist(bins=20, figsize=(15, 10))
plt.show()

# Step 4: Exclude non-numeric columns and normalize the data
non_numeric_columns = ['date', 'quarter', 'department', 'team', 'targeted_productivity', 'smv', 'day']
numeric_data = data.drop(['actual_productivity', 'class_label'] + non_numeric_columns, axis=1)
scaler = StandardScaler()
data_normalized = scaler.fit_transform(numeric_data)

# Step 5: Split the data into training and testing sets
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(data_normalized, data['class_label'], test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

# Checking the shape of the training and testing datasets
print("X_train shape:", X_train.shape)
print("X_test shape:", X_test.shape)
print("y_train shape:", y_train.shape)
print("y_test shape:", y_test.shape)

X_train shape: (957, 7)
X_test shape: (240, 7)
y_train shape: (957,)
y_test shape: (240,)
In[6]:
import numpy as np

def relu(x):
    """ReLU activation function."""
    return np.maximum(0, x)

def sigmoid(x):
    """Sigmoid activation function."""
    return 1 / (1 + np.exp(-x))

def sigmoid_derivative(x):
    """Derivative of the sigmoid activation function."""
    return sigmoid(x) * (1 - sigmoid(x))

def relu_derivative(x):
    """Derivative of the ReLU activation function."""
    return np.where(x > 0, 1, 0)

class NeuralNetwork:
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, output_size):
        # Initialize weights and biases
        self.W1 = np.random.randn(input_size, hidden_size)
        self.b1 = np.zeros((1, hidden_size))
        self.W2 = np.random.randn(hidden_size, output_size)
        self.b2 = np.zeros((1, output_size))

    def forward(self, X):
        # Forward propagation
        self.z1 = np.dot(X, self.W1) + self.b1
        self.a1 = np.tanh(self.z1)  # You can change this to ReLU if preferred
        self.z2 = np.dot(self.a1, self.W2) + self.b2
        self.output = self.sigmoid(self.z2)
        return self.output

    def backward(self, X, y, output, learning_rate):
        # Backpropagation
        m = X.shape[0]
        dz2 = output - y
        dW2 = (1 / m) * np.dot(self.a1.T, dz2)
        db2 = (1 / m) * np.sum(dz2, axis=0, keepdims=True)
        dz1 = np.dot(dz2, self.W2.T) * (1 - np.power(self.a1, 2))  # Derivative of tanh
        dW1 = (1 / m) * np.dot(X.T, dz1)
        db1 = (1 / m) * np.sum(dz1, axis=0, keepdims=True)

        # Update weights and biases
        self.W1 -= learning_rate * dW1
        self.b1 -= learning_rate * db1
        self.W2 -= learning_rate * dW2
        self.b2 -= learning_rate * db2

    def sigmoid(self, x):
        return 1 / (1 + np.exp(-x))

def compute_loss(output, y):
    m = y.shape[0]
    loss = -(1 / m) * np.sum(y * np.log(output) + (1 - y) * np.log(1 - output))
    return loss

# Create an instance of the NeuralNetwork class with updated architecture
input_size = X_train.shape[1]  # Updated to match the number of features
hidden_size = 8   # Updated to 8 hidden neurons
output_size = 1   # Binary classification

nn = NeuralNetwork(input_size, hidden_size, output_size)

# Define some sample input data (make sure it has the correct number of features)
sample_input = np.random.rand(1, input_size)  # Example with random values

# Forward propagate the sample input through the neural network
predicted_output = nn.forward(sample_input)

# Print the predicted output
print("Predicted output:", predicted_output)

In[5]:
# Outside the class
def compute_loss(output, y):
    m = y.shape[0]
    loss = -(1 / m) * np.sum(y * np.log(output) + (1 - y) * np.log(1 - output))
    return loss
In[8]:
# Define the number of epochs and the learning rate
epochs = 1000
learning_rate = 0.01  

# Training loop
for epoch in range(epochs):
    # Forward propagation
    output = nn.forward(X_train)
    
    # Compute the loss
    loss = compute_loss(output.flatten(), y_train)  # Flatten the output to have a 1-dimensional shape
    
    # Backpropagation
    nn.backward(X_train, y_train.values.reshape(-1, 1), output, learning_rate)
    
    # Print the loss every few epochs for tracking purposes
    if epoch % 100 == 0:
        print(f"Epoch {epoch}: Loss {loss}")
        
    # Print intermediate values
    if epoch % 100 == 0:
        print("Intermediate values:")
        print("Output:", output)
        print("Loss:", loss)

# Make predictions on the test set
y_pred = nn.forward(X_test).flatten()

# Convert predictions to binary labels
y_pred_binary = np.where(y_pred >= 0.5, 1, 0)

# Calculate evaluation metrics
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, roc_auc_score

accuracy = accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred_binary)
precision = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_binary)
recall = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_binary)
f1 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_binary)
roc_auc = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred)

# Print the results
print("Accuracy:", accuracy)
print("Precision:", precision)
print("Recall:", recall)
print("F1-score:", f1)
print("ROC AUC Score:", roc_auc)

In[10]:
# Define and train a neural network with 12 hidden neurons
nn_12 = NeuralNetwork(input_size=X_train.shape[1], hidden_size=12, output_size=1)
epochs = 1000
learning_rate = 0.01

# Training loop
for epoch in range(epochs):
    output = nn_12.forward(X_train)
    loss = compute_loss(output.flatten(), y_train)
    nn_12.backward(X_train, y_train.values.reshape(-1, 1), output, learning_rate)

# Predictions + evaluation
y_pred_train_12 = (nn_12.forward(X_train) > 0.5).astype(int)
y_pred_test_12 = (nn_12.forward(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

accuracy_12 = accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred_test_12)
precision_12 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_test_12)
recall_12 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_test_12)
f1_score_12 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_test_12)
roc_auc_12 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_test_12)

print(f"Performance with 12 hidden neurons:")
print(f"Accuracy: {accuracy_12}")
print(f"Precision: {precision_12}")
print(f"Recall: {recall_12}")
print(f"F1-score: {f1_score_12}")
print(f"ROC AUC Score: {roc_auc_12}")

# Define and train a neural network with 16 hidden neurons
nn_16 = NeuralNetwork(input_size=X_train.shape[1], hidden_size=16, output_size=1)
epochs = 1000
learning_rate = 0.01

# Training loop
for epoch in range(epochs):
    output = nn_16.forward(X_train)
    loss = compute_loss(output.flatten(), y_train)
    nn_16.backward(X_train, y_train.values.reshape(-1, 1), output, learning_rate)

# Predictions + evaluation
y_pred_train_16 = (nn_16.forward(X_train) > 0.5).astype(int)
y_pred_test_16 = (nn_16.forward(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

accuracy_16 = accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred_test_16)
precision_16 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_test_16)
recall_16 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_test_16)
f1_score_16 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_test_16)
roc_auc_16 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_test_16)

print(f"Recall: {recall_16}")

In[16]:
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras.models import Model
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Input, Dense
from tensorflow.keras.optimizers import Adam
from tensorflow.keras.losses import BinaryCrossentropy
from tensorflow.keras.metrics import AUC
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, roc_auc_score

# Create the input layer
input_layer = Input(shape=(X_train.shape[1],))

# Create the model with 12 hidden neurons
dense_layer1_12 = Dense(12, activation='relu')(input_layer)
output_layer_12 = Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')(dense_layer1_12)

# Combine input and output to create model
model_12 = Model(inputs=input_layer, outputs=output_layer_12)

# Compile the model
model_12.compile(optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=0.01), 
                 loss=BinaryCrossentropy(), 
                 metrics=['accuracy', AUC(name='auc')])

# Train the model
history_12 = model_12.fit(X_train, y_train, epochs=100, batch_size=10, validation_split=0.2, verbose=1)

# Evaluate the model
loss_12, accuracy_12, auc_12 = model_12.evaluate(X_test, y_test)
print(f'Accuracy (12 neurons): {accuracy_12}')
print(f'AUC (12 neurons): {auc_12}')

# Make predictions
y_pred_keras_12 = (model_12.predict(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

# Calculate other metrics
precision_keras_12 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
recall_keras_12 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
f1_score_keras_12 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
roc_auc_keras_12 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)

print(f'Precision (12 neurons): {precision_keras_12}')
print(f'Recall (12 neurons): {recall_keras_12}')
print(f'F1-score (12 neurons): {f1_score_keras_12}')
print(f'ROC AUC Score (12 neurons): {roc_auc_keras_12}')

# Create the model with 16 hidden neurons
dense_layer1_16 = Dense(16, activation='relu')(input_layer)
output_layer_16 = Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')(dense_layer1_16)

# Combine input and output to create model
model_16 = Model(inputs=input_layer, outputs=output_layer_16)

# Compile the model
model_16.compile(optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=0.01), 
                 loss=BinaryCrossentropy(), 
                 metrics=['accuracy', AUC(name='auc')])

# Train the model
history_16 = model_16.fit(X_train, y_train, epochs=100, batch_size=10, validation_split=0.2, verbose=1)

# Evaluate the model
loss_16, accuracy_16, auc_16 = model_16.evaluate(X_test, y_test)
print(f'Accuracy (16 neurons): {accuracy_16}')
print(f'AUC (16 neurons): {auc_16}')

# Make predictions
y_pred_keras_16 = (model_16.predict(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

# Calculate other metrics
precision_keras_16 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
recall_keras_16 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
f1_score_keras_16 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
roc_auc_keras_16 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)

print(f'Precision (16 neurons): {precision_keras_16}')
print(f'Recall (16 neurons): {recall_keras_16}')
print(f'F1-score (16 neurons): {f1_score_keras_16}')
print(f'ROC AUC Score (16 neurons): {roc_auc_keras_16}')

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense, InputLayer
from tensorflow.keras.optimizers import Adam
from tensorflow.keras.losses import BinaryCrossentropy
from tensorflow.keras.metrics import AUC
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, roc_auc_score

# Load the dataset
url = "https://archive.ics.uci.edu/ml/machine-learning-databases/00597/garments_worker_productivity.csv"
data = pd.read_csv(url)

# Handle missing values
data['wip'] = data['wip'].fillna(data['wip'].mean())

# Transform the target variable into a binary class label
threshold = 0.7  # Threshold for satisfactory productivity
data['class_label'] = np.where(data['actual_productivity'] >= threshold, 1, 0)

# Function to visualize feature distributions
def show_histograms(data):
    data.hist(bins=20, figsize=(15, 10))
    plt.show()

# Call this function only if you want to see the histograms
# show_histograms(data)  # Uncomment to display the histograms

# Exclude non-numeric columns and normalize the data
non_numeric_columns = ['date', 'quarter', 'department', 'team', 'targeted_productivity', 'smv', 'day']
numeric_data = data.drop(['actual_productivity', 'class_label'] + non_numeric_columns, axis=1)
scaler = StandardScaler()
data_normalized = scaler.fit_transform(numeric_data)

# Split the data into training and testing sets
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(data_normalized, data['class_label'], test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

# Define a function to create a model
def create_model(hidden_neurons):
    model = Sequential()
    model.add(InputLayer(shape=(X_train.shape[1],)))  # Use `shape` instead of `input_shape`
    model.add(Dense(hidden_neurons, activation='relu'))
    model.add(Dense(1, activation='sigmoid'))

    # Compile the model
    model.compile(optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=0.01), 
                  loss=BinaryCrossentropy(), 
                  metrics=['accuracy', AUC(name='auc')])
    return model

# Model with 12 hidden neurons
model_12 = create_model(12)
history_12 = model_12.fit(X_train, y_train, epochs=100, batch_size=10, validation_split=0.2, verbose=1)

# Evaluate the model
loss_12, accuracy_12, auc_12 = model_12.evaluate(X_test, y_test)
print(f'12 Neurons - Accuracy: {accuracy_12}, AUC: {auc_12}')

# Predictions
y_pred_keras_12 = (model_12.predict(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

# Metrics
precision_keras_12 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
recall_keras_12 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
f1_score_keras_12 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)
roc_auc_keras_12 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_12)

print(f'12 Neurons - Precision: {precision_keras_12}, Recall: {recall_keras_12}, F1-score: {f1_score_keras_12}, ROC AUC Score: {roc_auc_keras_12}')

# Model with 16 hidden neurons
model_16 = create_model(16)
history_16 = model_16.fit(X_train, y_train, epochs=100, batch_size=10, validation_split=0.2, verbose=1)

# Evaluate the model
loss_16, accuracy_16, auc_16 = model_16.evaluate(X_test, y_test)
print(f'16 Neurons - Accuracy: {accuracy_16}, AUC: {auc_16}')

# Predictions
y_pred_keras_16 = (model_16.predict(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)

# Metrics
precision_keras_16 = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
recall_keras_16 = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
f1_score_keras_16 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)
roc_auc_keras_16 = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_keras_16)

print(f'16 Neurons - Precision: {precision_keras_16}, Recall: {recall_keras_16}, F1-score: {f1_score_keras_16}, ROC AUC Score: {roc_auc_keras_16}')

# Results comparison
results = {
    "Hidden Neurons": [8, 12, 16],
    "Accuracy": [0.695833, accuracy_12, accuracy_16],
    "Precision": [0.716814, precision_keras_12, precision_keras_16],
    "Recall": [0.947368, recall_keras_12, recall_keras_16],
    "F1-score": [0.816121, f1_score_keras_12, f1_score_keras_16],
    "ROC AUC Score": [0.627045, roc_auc_keras_12, roc_auc_keras_16]
}

results_df = pd.DataFrame(results)
print(results_df)

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, roc_auc_score
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense, Input
from tensorflow.keras.optimizers import Adam

# Step 1: Load the dataset
url = "https://archive.ics.uci.edu/ml/machine-learning-databases/00597/garments_worker_productivity.csv"
data = pd.read_csv(url)

# Handle missing values
data['wip'] = data['wip'].fillna(data['wip'].mean())

# Step 2: Transform the target variable into a binary class label
threshold = 0.7  # Threshold for satisfactory productivity
data['class_label'] = np.where(data['actual_productivity'] >= threshold, 1, 0)

# Step 4: Exclude non-numeric columns and normalize the data
non_numeric_columns = ['date', 'quarter', 'department', 'team', 'targeted_productivity', 'smv', 'day']
numeric_data = data.drop(['actual_productivity', 'class_label'] + non_numeric_columns, axis=1)
scaler = StandardScaler()
data_normalized = scaler.fit_transform(numeric_data)

# Step 5: Split the data into training and testing sets
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(data_normalized, data['class_label'], test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

# Function to train and evaluate a neural network model
def train_evaluate_nn(hidden_neurons):
    # Define the model with an explicit Input layer
    model = Sequential([
        Input(shape=(X_train.shape[1],)),
        Dense(hidden_neurons, activation='relu'),
        Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')
    ])

    # Compile the model
    model.compile(optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=0.01), 
                  loss='binary_crossentropy', 
                  metrics=['accuracy'])

    # Train the model
    model.fit(X_train, y_train, epochs=100, batch_size=10, validation_split=0.2, verbose=0)

    # Evaluate the model
    loss, accuracy = model.evaluate(X_test, y_test, verbose=0)
    y_pred = (model.predict(X_test) > 0.5).astype(int)
    
    # Calculate additional metrics
    precision = precision_score(y_test, y_pred)
    recall = recall_score(y_test, y_pred)
    f1 = f1_score(y_test, y_pred)
    roc_auc = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred)

    return accuracy, precision, recall, f1, roc_auc

# Train and evaluate neural network models with different hidden neurons
results = []
for neurons in [8, 12, 16]:
    accuracy, precision, recall, f1, roc_auc = train_evaluate_nn(neurons)
    results.append({
        'Hidden Neurons': neurons,
        'Accuracy': accuracy,
        'Precision': precision,
        'Recall': recall,
        'F1-score': f1,
        'ROC AUC Score': roc_auc
    })

# Convert results to a DataFrame for easy viewing
nn_results_df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# Step 6: Train and evaluate a Random Forest model
# Initialize the Random Forest model
rf_model = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)

# Train the model
rf_model.fit(X_train, y_train)

# Predict on the test set
y_pred_rf = rf_model.predict(X_test)

# Evaluate the Random Forest model
accuracy_rf = accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred_rf)
precision_rf = precision_score(y_test, y_pred_rf)
recall_rf = recall_score(y_test, y_pred_rf)
f1_rf = f1_score(y_test, y_pred_rf)
roc_auc_rf = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_pred_rf)

# Print results for neural networks
print("\nNeural Network Model Performance:")
print(nn_results_df)

# Random Forest Model Performance
print(f"\nRandom Forest Model Performance:")
print(f"Accuracy: {accuracy_rf:.4f}")
print(f"Precision: {precision_rf:.4f}")
print(f"Recall: {recall_rf:.4f}")
print(f"F1 Score: {f1_rf:.4f}")
print(f"ROC AUC Score: {roc_auc_rf:.4f}")

# Compare the best neural network model to Random Forest
best_nn_model = nn_results_df.loc[nn_results_df['Accuracy'].idxmax()]
print(f"\nBest Neural Network Model with {best_nn_model['Hidden Neurons']} Hidden Neurons:")
print(f"Accuracy: {best_nn_model['Accuracy']:.4f}")
print(f"Precision: {best_nn_model['Precision']:.4f}")
print(f"Recall: {best_nn_model['Recall']:.4f}")
print(f"F1 Score: {best_nn_model['F1-score']:.4f}")
print(f"ROC AUC Score: {best_nn_model['ROC AUC Score']:.4f}")

# Calculate improvements
accuracy_improvement = best_nn_model['Accuracy'] - accuracy_rf
precision_improvement = best_nn_model['Precision'] - precision_rf
recall_improvement = best_nn_model['Recall'] - recall_rf
f1_improvement = best_nn_model['F1-score'] - f1_rf
roc_auc_improvement = best_nn_model['ROC AUC Score'] - roc_auc_rf

print(f"\nComparison of Best Neural Network and Random Forest Models:")
print(f"Accuracy Improvement: {accuracy_improvement:.4f}")
print(f"Precision Improvement: {precision_improvement:.4f}")
print(f"Recall Improvement: {recall_improvement:.4f}")
print(f"F1 Score Improvement: {f1_improvement:.4f}")
print(f"ROC AUC Score Improvement: {roc_auc_improvement:.4f}")

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Metrics for Random Forest Model
rf_accuracy = 0.8125
rf_precision = 0.8750
rf_recall = 0.8596
rf_f1 = 0.8673
rf_roc_auc = 0.7777

# Metrics for Neural Network Model with 8 hidden neurons
nn_8_accuracy = 0.766667
nn_8_precision = 0.870968
nn_8_recall = 0.789474
nn_8_f1 = 0.828221
nn_8_roc_auc = 0.749809

# Metrics for Neural Network Model with 12 hidden neurons
nn_12_accuracy = 0.7875
nn_12_precision = 0.819149
nn_12_recall = 0.900585
nn_12_f1 = 0.857939
nn_12_roc_auc = 0.703916

# Metrics for Neural Network Model with 16 hidden neurons
nn_16_accuracy = 0.7875
nn_16_precision = 0.803030
nn_16_recall = 0.929825
nn_16_f1 = 0.861789
nn_16_roc_auc = 0.682304

# Performance metrics lists
metrics = ['Accuracy', 'Precision', 'Recall', 'F1-score', 'ROC AUC Score']
rf_metrics = [rf_accuracy, rf_precision, rf_recall, rf_f1, rf_roc_auc]
nn_8_metrics = [nn_8_accuracy, nn_8_precision, nn_8_recall, nn_8_f1, nn_8_roc_auc]
nn_12_metrics = [nn_12_accuracy, nn_12_precision, nn_12_recall, nn_12_f1, nn_12_roc_auc]
nn_16_metrics = [nn_16_accuracy, nn_16_precision, nn_16_recall, nn_16_f1, nn_16_roc_auc]

# Create the line plot
plt.figure(figsize=(12, 7))
plt.plot(metrics, rf_metrics, marker='o', label='Random Forest')
plt.plot(metrics, nn_8_metrics, marker='o', label='Neural Network (8 hidden neurons)')
plt.plot(metrics, nn_12_metrics, marker='o', label='Neural Network (12 hidden neurons)')
plt.plot(metrics, nn_16_metrics, marker='o', label='Neural Network (16 hidden neurons)')
plt.title('Performance Metrics Comparison')
plt.xlabel('Metrics')
plt.ylabel('Score')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.xticks(rotation=45)
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()
